***kneu.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kneu.html>kneu</a> (104246)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cnuut</i>, <span class="Latn" lang="dum">cnuyt</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">jackdaw, crow</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cnoteren</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cnueteren</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cneuteren</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to twitter</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Equivalent to an apocope of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">kneuter</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kneu.html>kneu</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> or <abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kneus.html>kneus</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kneu.html>kneutje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>common linnet, <i>Linaria cannabina</i>

***kneus.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kneus.html>kneus</a> (23789)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kneuzen.html>kneuzen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to hurt, <a href = vnd.unilang:bruisen.html>bruise</a>, grind</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kneus.html>kneus</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kneuzen.html>kneuzen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kneusje.html>kneusje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A <a href = vnd.unilang:bruisen.html>bruise</a>, hurt body part (notably skin) without an open wound</li>
<li>A bruised egg</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A violation, infraction</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> An inferior worker, unproductive winer</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Any weakling, <a href = vnd.unilang:softie.html>softie</a></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>(<a href = vnd.unilang:bruisen.html>bruise</a>) <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:blauwe.html>blauwe</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:plek.html>plek</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kneuzing.html>kneuzing</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl">kneuswond</span>(e), <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kwetsuur.html>kwetsuur</a></span></li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kneus.html>kneus</a></strong>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knie.html>knie</a> (4655)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cnie</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*cnio</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*knewą</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*ǵónu</i>.

</p>
<ol><li>A knee.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">chiefly diminutive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A kneeing, a prod or blow with the knee.</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:knielen.html>knielen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*kniolon</i>. Ultimately derived from <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knie.html>knie</a></i>, but the source of the <i>l</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> unknown.

</p>

***knijpen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knijpen.html>knijpen</a> (6846)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">knipen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*knīpen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*knīpaną</i>. Likely related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">nijpen</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knijpen.html>knijpen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to pinch, squeeze</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:knijpen.html>knijpen</a></b>
</p>

***knikken.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knikken.html>knikken</a> (15802)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cnicken</i>; related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:neigen.html>neigen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to bend, turn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">nicken</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to nod</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, itself from <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:neigen.html>neigen</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knikken.html>knikken</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>to nod as in to express agreement.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:knikken.html>knikken</a></b>

***knikker.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knikker.html>knikker</a> (19182)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knikken.html>knikken</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*knikkoną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to fold, <a href = vnd.unilang:snap.html>snap</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> imitative.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knikker.html>knikker</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knikkers.html>knikkers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knikker.html>knikkertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a marble <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">toy</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li>various similarly shaped <a href = vnd.unilang:objects.html>objects</a>, including:
<ol><li>a billiards ball</li>
<li>certain seeds</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">humorous</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a head, especially a bald skull (typically in <i><a href = vnd.unilang:kale.html>kale</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:knikker.html>knikker</a></i>)</li></ol></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> a lump or stone</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">metonymically</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <i>(in the plural, absolutely used with definite article: <b><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:knikkers.html>knikkers</a></b>)</i> The stakes of a game, deal etc.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><a href = vnd.unilang:marbles.html>marbles</a></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">marbel</span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:stuiter.html>stuiter</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Germanic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:Germanic languages">Germanic</a></span>: the root of <a href = vnd.unilang:knikken.html>knikken</a> 'to nod' + <a href = vnd.unilang:dictatoriaal.html>-er</a>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knikker.html>knikker</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knikkers.html>knikkers</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knikker.html>knikkertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A nodder</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knikkers.html>knikkers</a> (19181)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knikkers.html>knikkers</a></strong>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knip.html>knip</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">wink</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:oog.html>oog</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">eye</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kniepauge</i>.
</p>

***knippen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knippen.html>knippen</a> (5101)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:knippen.html>knippen</a></i>, further etymology unknown. Directly related only with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Low German">Middle Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gml"><a href = vnd.unilang:knippen.html>knippen</a></i>. Probably onomatopoeic.
</p><p>The sense “to blink” may, at least in part, be due to conflation with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knijpen.html>knijpen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to squeeze</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a></i> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ogen.html>ogen</a></i> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">toeknijpen</i> (“to screw up one’s eyes”); also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:knippen.html>knippen</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">kniepen</i> both in the sense of “to blink”, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">kniepen</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knippen.html>knippen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cut with scissors</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> computing</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to cut (remove an item and place it in memory for <a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a> use)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make a pinching movement, especially with one's eyelids; thus, to blink</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to <a href = vnd.unilang:snap.html>snap</a> one's <a href = vnd.unilang:fingers.html>fingers</a></li></ol>

***knobbel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knobbel.html>knobbel</a> (42071)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">knobbe</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*knappô</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">button</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.  Compare regional German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Knubbel</i> as well as <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Knopf</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">button</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knobbel.html>knobbel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knobbels.html>knobbels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knobbel.html>knobbeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>knob, knot, lump</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> an aptitude for something</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">knofloick</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">knuuflooch</i>, a dissimilated variant of earlier <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cloffloc</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span>literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">clove-leek</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:klieven.html>klieven</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">look</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Knoblauch</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">knyflok</i> and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">clove</i>.

***knokkel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knokkel.html>knokkel</a> (74914)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cnokel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*knukil</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*knukilaz</i>, a diminutive of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*knukô</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bone</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (whence <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">knook</i>). Thus, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> synchronically equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">knook</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bone</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-el</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="ann-pos">diminutive suffix</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">knuckle</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Knöchel</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Knochen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">kno</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">knoge</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knokkel.html>knokkel</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knokkel.html>knokkels</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knokkel.html>knokkeltje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>finger-joint; knuckle</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">vingergewricht</span></li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

***knoll.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knoll.html>knoll</a> (74911)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">cnoll</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">summit</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*knudan-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*knudla-</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*knulla-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">lump</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, possibly related to <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">cnotta</i>.
</p><p>Related to Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">knollr</i> (found only in names of <a href = vnd.unilang:places.html>places</a>), Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knol.html>knol</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tuber</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Swedish <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">knöl</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">tuber</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Danish <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">knold</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">hillock, clod, tuber</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> and German <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Knolle</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bulb</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:knoll.html>knoll</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">knolls</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A small mound or rounded hill.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1813</b>,  <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Walter_Scott" class="extiw" title="w:Walter Scott"><a href = vnd.unilang:walter.html>Walter</a> Scott</a>,  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Rokeby" class="extiw" title="w:Rokeby">Rokeby</a></cite>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">On <b><a href = vnd.unilang:knoll.html>knoll</a></b> or hillock rears his crest, / Lonely and huge, the giant oak.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2008</b> January–February,  <a href = vnd.unilang:matt.html>Matt</a> Bean,  “Your cultural calendar: 7 <a href = vnd.unilang:things.html>things</a> to look forward to this year”, in  <cite><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Men%27s_Health" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Men | s Health"><a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>Men</a>'s Health</a></cite>, volume 23, number 1, <small><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/International_Standard_Serial_Number" class="extiw" title="w:International Standard Serial Number">ISSN</a> <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://www.worldcat.org/issn/1054-4836">1054-4836</a></small>, page <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="https://books.google.com/books?id=6ccDAAAAMBAJamp;pg=PA135amp;dq=%22knoll%22">135</a>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">In the northern hemisphere, June 21 <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> the most daylight <a href = vnd.unilang:hours.html>hours</a>. Pack a picnic—a chilled bottle of Sancerre, cheese, olives, and a nice baguette—and hit the grassy <b><a href = vnd.unilang:knoll.html>knoll</a></b>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Imitative, or variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">knell</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:knoll.html>knoll</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">knolls</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A knell.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:knoll.html>knoll</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">knolls</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">knolling</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">knolled</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To <a href = vnd.unilang:ring.html>ring</a> (a bell) mournfully; to knell.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To sound, like a bell; to knell.
<ul><li><i>c</i>. <b>1599</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/William_Shakespeare" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:William Shakespeare">William Shakespeare</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/As_You_Like_It" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:As You Like It">As You Like It</a></i>, Act II, scene VII, 114
<dl><dd>If ever <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> where bells have <b>knoll´d</b> to church.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>1815</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Lord_Byron" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Lord Byron">Lord Byron</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Works_of_Lord_Byron_(ed._Coleridge,_Prothero)/Poetry/Volume_3/Parisina" class="extiw" title="s:The Works of Lord Byron (ed. Coleridge, Prothero)/Poetry/Volume 3/Parisina">Parisina</a></i>
<dl><dd>For a departed being's soul / The death hymn peals, and the hollow bells <b><a href = vnd.unilang:knoll.html>knoll</a></b>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>?</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Alfred_Tennyson" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Alfred Tennyson">Alfred Tennyson</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikisource.org/wiki/The_Gardener%27s_Daughter;_or,_the_Pictures" class="extiw" title="s:The Gardener | s Daughter; or, the Pictures">The Gardener's Daughter; or, The Pictures</a></i>
<dl><dd>Heavy clocks <b>knolling</b> the drowsy <a href = vnd.unilang:hours.html>hours</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Named after <a href = vnd.unilang:knoll.html>Knoll</a>, a furniture fabrication shop, famous for its angular range of designer furniture.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:knoll.html>knoll</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">knolls</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">knolling</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">knolled</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To arrange related <a href = vnd.unilang:objects.html>objects</a> in parallel or at 90 degree angles.</li></ol>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knolraap.html>knolraap</a> (82098)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knol.html>knol</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bulb</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:raap.html>raap</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">rape, turnip</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knolraap.html>knolraap</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knolraap.html>knolrapen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knolraap.html>knolraapje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>turnip, cultivated plant with edible white root, <i>Brassica <a href = vnd.unilang:rapa.html>rapa</a></i></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:knolraap.html>knolraap</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span>/<span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:plantkunde.html>plantkunde</a>)</span>, <span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:groente.html>groente</a>)</span> <a href="https://species.wikimedia.org/wiki/Brassica_rapa" class="extiw" title="wikispecies:Brassica rapa"><span style="color:green;"><i>Brassica <a href = vnd.unilang:rapa.html>rapa</a></i></span></a> <img alt="op Wikispecies" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/14px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png" decoding="async" width="14" height="18" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/21px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Wikispecies-logo-en.png/28px-Wikispecies-logo-en.png 2x" data-file-width="125" data-file-height="160" /> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:eetbaar.html>eetbare</a> knolsoort</li></ol>

***knoop.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knoop.html>knoop</a> (4914)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">cnôop</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*knōp</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*knaupaz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Knauf</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knoop.html>knoop</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knopen.html>knopen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knoopje.html>knoopje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>button (knob or small disc serving as a fastener)</li>
<li>knot (i.e. a <a href = vnd.unilang:loop.html>loop</a> of string or any other long flexible material which cannot be untied without pulling part of the string through the <a href = vnd.unilang:loops.html>loops</a>)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zit.html>zit</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:knoop.html>knoop</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I'm in a hard spot. / I'm all tied up.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> knot</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">nautical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> knot (i.e. a unit of velocity, corresponding to traveling a distance of 1 nautical mile per hour)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">botany</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> node, joint</li></ol>

***knop.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knop.html>knop</a> (3261)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Knopf</i> and probably <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:knop.html>knop</a></i>. Also related with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">knob</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knobbel.html>knobbel</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Knubbel</i>, which are cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">knob</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knop.html>knop</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knoppen.html>knoppen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knopje.html>knopje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a knob, roundish handle, ornament etc.</li>
<li>a button, control device to push etc.; metonymy: control, power to <a href = vnd.unilang:stop.html>stop</a></li>
<li>a <a href = vnd.unilang:bud.html>bud</a> on a (growing) plant</li></ol>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:knorren.html>knorren</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to grunt like a pig, to grumble like a hungry stomach</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<p>A word that rapidly <a href = vnd.unilang:came.html>came</a> into fashion in the 1920s. Probably related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">kneuter</i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">kneuterig</i>.

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:knuffelen.html>knuffelen</a> (7048)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Unknown. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">knuffeln</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">knüffeln</i>, an iterative form of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">knuffen</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to poke; bump; nudge</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">knoffelje</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to push; knock; bump</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Netherlands" class="extiw" title="w:Netherlands">Netherlands</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A stupid, silly person; a buffoon

***kobalt.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:kobalt.html>kobalt</a> (35946)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:kobalt.html>Kobalt</a></i>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:kobold.html>Kobold</a></i>, originally an derogatory nickname for the 'inferior' ore which contaminated silver finds.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_5">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kobalt.html>kobalt</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>The metallic element and material cobalt</li>
<li>The <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> made from its oxyde</li>
<li>Its bluish metallic color shade</li></ol>

<p>18th century. Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:kobold.html>Kobold</a></i>. <head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:koe.html>koe</a> (2965)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">coe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">cuo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kūz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʷṓws</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">cow</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">ko</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds"><a href = vnd.unilang:koh.html>Koh</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Kuh</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Luxembourgish" class="extiw" title="w:Luxembourgish">Luxembourgish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="lb"><a href = vnd.unilang:kou.html>Kou</a></i>, and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">ko</i>.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:koek.html>koek</a> (10667)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">coeke</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*kuoko</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*kōkô</i>.

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koekblik.html>koekblik</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koekblikken.html>koekblikken</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koekblik.html>koekblikje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>biscuit tin <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">metal container for <a href = vnd.unilang:biscuits.html>biscuits</a>, cake, <a href = vnd.unilang:cookies.html>cookies</a>, etc.</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>

***koekeloeren.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:koekeloeren.html>koekeloeren</a> (64382)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">kokeloer</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">kokerol</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">snail</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">coque</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">large hollow shell</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koekeloeren.html>koekeloeren</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">informal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To look, to <a href = vnd.unilang:staren.html>stare</a>.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:loeren.html>loeren</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:staren.html>staren</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to idle, to be somewhere without doing much.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:staat.html>Staat</a> 'm <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weer.html>weer</a> wa' <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hangen.html>hangen</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:koekeloeren.html>koekeloeren</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> '<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> hoekske | <a href = vnd.unilang:niks.html>niks</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:beters.html>beters</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:te.html>te</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a>!</i><dl><dd><small>(please add an English translation of this usage example)</small></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">geelogen</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Possibly onomatopoeic. Compare <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kukeleku.html>kukeleku</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:koekeloeren.html>koekeloeren</a></strong>
</p>
